	if (!String.prototype.startsWith) {
		String.prototype.startsWith = function(searchString, position) {
			position = position || 0;
			return this.indexOf(searchString, position) === position;
		};
	}
	if (!String.prototype.includes) {
		String.prototype.includes = function() {
			'use strict';

		};

			var i;
			var len = this.length;

			thisArg = thisArg || window;

			for ( i = 0; i < len; i++ ) {
				callback.call( thisArg, this[ i ], i, this );
			}
		};

				case 'social':

				return '<style>.cmp-placeholder-box{text-align:center !important;padding:1% 1% 5% 1% !important;background-color:#fff !important;border:1px solid #F2F2F2 !important}.cmp-placeholder-item{margin:2.5% 0 !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-privacy-link{text-align:right !important;margin: .5% 1% 0 0 !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-text{font-size:14px !important;color:#000 !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-button{background:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) linear-gradient(to bottom, #0c5798 0, #2f72ac 100%) repeat scroll 0 0 !important;border-radius:3px !important;color:white !important;cursor:pointer !important;padding:5px !important;text-align:center !important;font-size:16px !important;padding: .75% 1.5% !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-button:hover{background:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) linear-gradient(to bottom, #2f72ac 0, #0c5798 100%) repeat scroll 0 0 !important;color:white !important;text-decoration:none !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-headline{font-size:25px !important;font-weight:bold !important}.cmp-placeholder-item.cmp-placeholder-text-small{font-size:10px !important;color:#808080 !important}</style><div class="cmp-placeholder-box"><div class="cmp-placeholder-item cmp-placeholder-privacy-link cmp-placeholder-text-small">Datenschutzhinweis</div><div class="cmp-placeholder-item cmp-placeholder-headline">Externer Inhalt</div><div class="cmp-placeholder-item cmp-placeholder-text"> An dieser Stelle finden Sie einen eingebetteten externen Inhalt z.B. von einem sozialen Netzwerk oder einem unserer Partner.<br /> Zum Anzeigen aktivieren Sie bitte "<strong>Externe Inhalte / Soziale Netzwerke</strong>" in den Privatsphäre-Einstellungen.</div><div class="cmp-placeholder-item cmp-placeholder-text-small"> Mit der Aktivierung erklären Sie sich einverstanden, dass Ihnen externe Inhalte angezeigt werden. Dabei können u.U. auch personenbezogene Daten an Drittplattformen übermittelt werden.</div> <a class="cmp-placeholder-item cmp-placeholder-button" onclick="_cmp_.showPM()">Privatsphäre-Einstellungen öffnen </a></div>';
			}
		},

		base64Decode: function base64Decode(encodedData) {
			var decodeUTF8string = function decodeUTF8string(str) {
				return str.split('').map(function (c) {
					var transformedVal = '%' + ('00' + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2);

					try {
						return decodeURIComponent(transformedVal);
					} catch (error) {
						console.group();
						console.log('[CMP] error in decodeUTF8string - val ' + c + ' transformed to ' + transformedVal);
						console.log(error);
						console.groupEnd();
						return '';
					}
				}).join('');
			};

			if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
				if (typeof window.atob !== 'undefined') {
					return decodeUTF8string(window.atob(encodedData));
				}
			} else {
				return new Buffer(encodedData, 'base64').toString('utf-8');
			}

			var b64 = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/=';
			var o1;
			var o2;
			var o3;
			var h1;
			var h2;
			var h3;
			var h4;
			var bits;
			var i = 0;
			var ac = 0;
			var dec = '';
			var tmpArr = [];

			if (!encodedData) {
				return encodedData;
			}

			encodedData += '';

			do {
				h1 = b64.indexOf(encodedData.charAt(i++));
				h2 = b64.indexOf(encodedData.charAt(i++));
				h3 = b64.indexOf(encodedData.charAt(i++));
				h4 = b64.indexOf(encodedData.charAt(i++));

				bits = h1 << 18 | h2 << 12 | h3 << 6 | h4;

				o1 = bits >> 16 & 0xff;
				o2 = bits >> 8 & 0xff;
				o3 = bits & 0xff;

				if (h3 === 64) {
					tmpArr[ac++] = String.fromCharCode(o1);
				} else if (h4 === 64) {
					tmpArr[ac++] = String.fromCharCode(o1, o2);
				} else {
					tmpArr[ac++] = String.fromCharCode(o1, o2, o3);
				}
			} while (i < encodedData.length);

			dec = tmpArr.join('');
			return decodeUTF8string(dec.replace(/\0+$/, ''));
		}
	};

	function addVendor(vendor, id) {
		_cmp_.addVendor(vendor, id);
	}

	function removeVendor(vendor, id) {
		_cmp_.removeVendor(vendor, id);
	}

	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var cookie = new Cookie();

  
  $(document).ready(function() {
    var expirationDay = 365;

    cookie.key = "cookieOverlayAgreed";
    cookie.value = "true";
    cookie.domain = ".finanzen.ch";
    cookie.path = "/";
    cookie.expires = expirationDay * 86400000;

    locateIP()
      .then(function(promise) {
        if (promise.country_code == 'DE' || promise.country_code == 'AT') {
          closeOverlay();
        }
        else if (cookie.isSet()) {
          closeOverlay();
        } else {
          showOverlay();
        }
      });
      IIRFilterNode
      // .catch(function(error) {
      //   console.error(error);
      // });
  });


	function buttonClick() {
		cookie.setCookie();
		closeOverlay();
	}

	function closeOverlay() {
		$("#cookie-overlay").hide();
	}
	function showOverlay() {
		$("#cookie-overlay").show();
	}
</script>
